The room was on the second floor, so there was no view of the lake. It was a bit noisy when the bus stopped below, but it didn't affect much.
The twin room was super big. It felt like 4 adults could stay there without any pressure. There were 2 air conditioners in the room, which was very comfortable.
The bathroom was Bulgari, which was still very high-end. The overall hardware facilities were very good (except that it was not only a toilet).
The hotel has a super large children's playground, comparable to Nelbao, with sand digging, trampolines, carousels, slides, supermarkets, climbing frames, etc. It is definitely the first choice for children. The children refused to come out in it, and the staff inside were very friendly. The carousel was open at a fixed time. If the children missed the time period, they could discuss with the staff. If there were other children who wanted to sit, they could accommodate them.
Because our room couldn't see the lake view, we went to the executive lounge on the 7th floor for afternoon tea. The taste was okay. There was an event on 618, the price was also very good, and the waiters were very good. We said we wanted to watch the sunset, and they enthusiastically told us that it would be better to go after 6pm. However, the sun set late that day, and we really didn't want to wait until 6:30, so we had to go for dinner. The breakfast variety was OK. Their homemade Qiandao Lake yogurt was very good. Although we went on a weekday, there were still many people at breakfast. We were given a small gift when we left the hotel. The housekeeper Xiaofen also provided good service and responded to every request. The downside was that they didn't contact me in advance. I didn't know that the water park was open, and I didn't bring a swimsuit and a swimming ring for the children. The hotel built such a large children's park, which must be the main focus of parent-child activities. In this regard, the supplies in the room can be improved. In addition to children's toothpaste, toothbrush, slippers and bathrobes, children's mouthwash cups, children's toilets, etc. are also recommended. If the number is limited, it is recommended to list them in the room in advance. If necessary, you can contact the front desk or the housekeeper, which is better. Overall, it is good and I will consider staying in the future. If you don't go to the attractions, it is a good place to lie flat and walk your baby for 2 days in the hotel.

msg:A parent-child hotel that is super suitable for traveling with children
First of all, the location is very good. Although it is not a sea view alone, it is only separated from the lake by a road, and there is no obstruction to the lake from the fourth floor and above. In addition, it is only a three- to five-minute walk from the famous Fish Street. There is everything you want to eat, and you don‚Äôt have to go to a distant place to eat.
The second is that the hotel has a good view. Whether you live on the side of the lake view room or not, there is a large platform where you can see the Qiandao Lake view you want to see at any time. You can move a chair and lay a yoga mat to enjoy the scenery comfortably. The inner courtyard of the hotel is also very large, with a nine-curve corridor and a fish pond. Children like to watch groups of fish wandering around, and there is also a small hill that is not too high.
The third is that the parent-child park is really big. On B1 of the hotel, one side is the video game area and the other side is the parent-child park. There are supermarket shopping areas, gas stations, police stations and other role-playing landscapes, as well as a huge trampoline area, ocean balls, sand digging, and surprisingly, there is also a cute pet area. The child stayed for four days and didn‚Äôt play all the projects.
The fourth is that the breakfast category is very complete. The breakfast meets the five-star standard, with both Chinese and Western food, and even a children's dining area - the cakes are made into cartoon shapes, equipped with handrails and ladders so that children can take their own meals, and there are enough children's plates and tableware.
The fifth is good butler service. Before arriving at the store, the butler Xiaozhe informed me of the check-in details one by one, and asked me if I needed help every day. The room where the children live specially helped to install the bed guard, and also arranged children's bathrobes, slippers, toiletries, etc., which is really considerate. Free shoe covers are also distributed at the entrance of the parent-child park, two pairs of adults and a child. The young ladies in the park also take good care of the children and pay attention to the safety of the children at all times. For example, Sister Xiao Huang and Sister Xiao Ling are very nice. The only drawback is that the hotel occupancy rate may be high recently, and the room service staff is too tight. There were two days when the room was cleaned late in the afternoon.
Suggestions on room selection. High floors are better than low floors. The lake view room faces Qiandao Lake without any obstruction; the inner lake view room can see the hotel courtyard, the music lake view fountain and water curtain movie at 7:30 every night. In fact, I highly recommend the inner lake view room with a better cost-effectiveness. First of all, it is cheap, and secondly, it is very convenient to watch water curtain movies. If there are children, generally speaking, this kind of dynamic picture can attract their attention more than the endless and calm Thousand Island Lake view.
Some suggestions: The hotel's bathtub and bath water are very good, you can bring your own bath bag to enjoy it. The price of the hotel's main meal is high, and the average price per person in the surrounding good restaurants is not more than 100. The foot massage shop downstairs is more favorable. Don't use the coupons given by the hotel directly, so as not to be a sucker, but my family said that the massage is average. If there is free cycling time, it is recommended to take advantage of the rules to ride around, the scenery is good.
Some shortcomings: The hotel receives many groups, and there are many people when you go to eat. The air conditioner blows directly on the bed, and the air conditioner baffle can be provided. The gym and swimming pool were not used at all. It was a pity that they were repaired during those days. Although the parent-child park is disinfected and cleaned three times a day, the ground is still very dirty. Looking forward to improvement.

msg:I have been to Qiandao Lake about three or four times. The last time was eight or nine years ago. At that time, there was no high-speed rail. You either drove for four or five hours or took a bus.

I stayed at Hilton Binjiang several times before, which was already very beautiful. I didn't expect to stay at Minghao this time. The waves beat the waves.

Minghao has been open for several years. Since its opening, it has actually been in my favorites. I have never had the opportunity to come. This time I finally got the chance to come. I was not disappointed and the experience was excellent.

First of all, I would like to praise the housekeeper Miss Dong (Jane Dong) this time. After adding WeChat the night before check-in, she sent me a detailed arrangement of the hotel's activities during the May Day holiday, as well as the hotel's restaurants and the opening schedule of various facilities. After communication, I found that we were with a young child, and they helped upgrade a very good room. The floor was high and the view was good. I asked the guest room to put the bed together and add a fence in advance. After arriving in the room, I found that the children's bathrobes, toothbrushes, slippers, etc. were prepared in advance. Throughout the three-day and two-night trip, the hotel staff showed very high professionalism. Whether it was the staff at the entrance of the children's playground, the cleaning lady, the big brother of the concierge depar**ent, and of course the front desk staff, they were all polite, enthusiastic and polite, with some professionalism and dedication that even higher-end hotels may not have. This made me admire the hotel owner very much for being able to manage this team so well.

The hotel has many advantages. To be honest, I used to be a hotel employee, and I really like to experience hotels of different styles around the world. I am also a frequent visitor to chain hotels such as Hilton and Marriott, but this hotel really impressed me because it was so sincere, not only in terms of facilities (a guest room has three washbasins, including a low platform for children and a sink with adjustable faucets), aesthetics (peacock green washbasin bathtub with golden bronze partition faucet, there is a water curtain show at night, and jade sculpture screens can be seen everywhere in the public areas of the lobby), service (take Miss Dong as an example, there was an emergency at home, and she did not forget to ask the guests if they were satisfied with their stay and what they needed at night), children's playground (3,000 square meters of playground, only in Pu I have seen similar-sized hotels with large amusement parks in the Borui in Dong and Shangri-La in Sanya, and there are even cute pet parks and indoor and outdoor swimming pools, so luxurious!), breakfast (I plan to write about breakfast separately, because breakfast is also one of the most abundant hotels I have seen. Although it does not provide very high-end ingredients, such as the whole plate of honeycomb provided by the W Hotel in Singapore, and coconuts can be taken at will in several major hotels in Hainan, but they cost hundreds of yuan per person), and finally the price (the price is really low, the group purchase price is only 600-700 yuan, and the whole package includes the room, breakfast, and one-hour bicycle rental. The minibar is not just a few bottles of juice, but beer, Evian, and nut chocolate, and it also includes unlimited children's playground and 50 coins). .

I hope Minghao can open a chain, of course, the quality should not decline, I can really recommend this hotel, the cost performance is really very very very high!

  The room is large and hygienic (the toilet seat is electrically heated). My daughter said that the bed is very comfortable, like sleeping in the clouds. There is a large balcony where you can stay in a daze for a long time because the view of the lake is very good. beautiful.
  Room service is on call and your reasonable requests will be met in a timely manner. Butler Xiao Dong has excellent service. He communicated our room requirements in advance, carefully and patiently understood my needs. He is very kind and really helpful. Feel free to ask questions, feel free to answer. He also personally sent us upstairs to check in.
  Regarding service, everyone in the hotel takes it very seriously. To go to other floors in the hotel, you need to use the elevator card to swipe the floor. As a result, my friend can't get up to the one downstairs, and I can't get off the one upstairs. If I want to go , I need to go to the first floor to find help. (Will I be able to access 2 floors with one card in the future?) However, when I met the room service guy, he proactively discovered that I needed help in a timely manner and helped me check the elevator floor. He took the initiative to care about me. , and took the initiative to help solve the problem. I have not experienced this in other hotels, and it is still fresh in my memory.
  The breakfast at the hotel is the best breakfast I have ever had. Not only are there many varieties, but they also taste great. For example, those leek pancakes and radish pancakes are not pre-made products. They are made and fried on site, so the taste is natural. Very good, Huainan beef soup, I drank 3 bowls of clear soup in one go, and the large floor-to-ceiling glass windows in the dining area are quite beautiful, with small bridges, pavilions, and transparent fish ponds. While sitting and dining, You can enjoy such beautiful scenery and start the day in a good mood.
  On the ba*****t floor of the hotel, there is a large swimming pool and a gym. There are 2 table tennis tables at the door. Further inside, there is a children's playground of more than 3,000 square meters. Entry is free by swiping the room card, and non-slip socks are provided. The playground There is actually a small animal viewing area at the end of the park, and I can't help but wonder what's in it. Opposite the amu*****t park is the game machine room and go-kart driving. In the words of my daughter, it is so fun here that I don‚Äôt have enough time to play in a hurry.
  The location of the hotel is also very good. Just across the road when you go out is Fish Street, which is full of restaurants. There are many choices and they don't rip off customers. It only takes 3 kilometers to take a taxi to the pier, and you can get to the pier with the starting fee, which is very convenient.
  There is a dessert takeaway near the hotel that is delicious. When you order takeout at the hotel, it is delivered upstairs by a robot, which is very smart.
   To sum up, the hotel hardware (facilities) and software (services) are excellent, and the location is very good. I will definitely stay at Minghao next time I go to Qiandao Lake, and Xiaodong will welcome me.

It is very convenient to take a boat. There is a food stall next to the fish, and it is 300 meters away from the hotel. The decoration of the hotel is very luxurious. With seven landscapes, it can be compared to luxury hotels in Macau. The rooms are all marble paved, and even the toiletries are Bulgari. After staying in the hotel, I found that this is a hotel very suitable for parent-child travel. The hotel comes with 7,000 square meters A children's paradise, there are many items for children to play, and there are swimming pools, both outdoor and indoor. In the hotel, you can rent bicycles for free with your room card, and you can also buy fish food for 10 yuan to feed the fish. In the lobby at night You can watch water curtain movies everywhere; if you are obsessed with taking a boat, you can also rent a cruise at the hotel or buy tickets at the front desk, and hotel guests have discounts.

Having said so many advantages, let me talk about the disadvantages of the hotel. The room is basically quiet, but if there are children yelling in the corridor, you can hear it clearly. The side of the room that looks at Qiandao Lake is next to the road, so you can sit at night The balcony will be disturbed by the street lights; in addition, if you come by car, the parking location is at B1. When there are many guests, the parking space is still a little far away from the hotel elevator entrance. The parking lot, swimming pool, and children's playground are all on B1. different direction.

I am very grateful to the hotel manager Xiao Wang for his help. The staff are very nice, and I will recommend friends to check in in the future! This is really a hotel very suitable for parents and children~

Minghao is the only one I have lived in that has the air conditioner switch at hand, which is very user-friendly.
